	any_identifier	go to state 27
	path_segment	go to state 28
	assertion	go to state 32

	SYM_END_CBLOCK	shift, and go to state 441

state 440

	c_excludes  ->  SYM_EXCLUDE assertions .   (rule 49)
	assertions  ->  assertions . assertion   (rule 51)
	assertion  ->  . any_identifier ':' boolean_expression   (rule 52)
	assertion  ->  . boolean_expression   (rule 53)

	boolean_node  ->  . arithmetic_expression '=' arithmetic_expression   (rule 61)
	boolean_node  ->  . arithmetic_expression SYM_NE arithmetic_expression   (rule 62)
	boolean_node  ->  . arithmetic_expression SYM_LT arithmetic_expression   (rule 63)
	boolean_node  ->  . arithmetic_expression SYM_GT arithmetic_expression   (rule 64)
	boolean_node  ->  . arithmetic_expression SYM_LE arithmetic_expression   (rule 65)
	boolean_node  ->  . arithmetic_expression SYM_GE arithmetic_expression   (rule 66)
	boolean_node  ->  . boolean_expression SYM_AND boolean_expression   (rule 67)
	boolean_node  ->  . boolean_expression SYM_OR boolean_expression   (rule 68)
	boolean_node  ->  . boolean_expression SYM_XOR boolean_expression   (rule 69)
	boolean_node  ->  . boolean_expression SYM_IMPLIES boolean_expression   (rule 70)
	boolean_leaf  ->  . '(' boolean_expression ')'   (rule 71)
	boolean_leaf  ->  . SYM_TRUE   (rule 72)
	boolean_leaf  ->  . SYM_FALSE   (rule 73)
	arithmetic_expression  ->  . arithmetic_leaf   (rule 74)
	arithmetic_expression  ->  . arithmetic_node   (rule 75)
	arithmetic_node  ->  . arithmetic_expression '+' arithmetic_leaf   (rule 76)
	arithmetic_node  ->  . arithmetic_expression '-' arithmetic_leaf   (rule 77)
	arithmetic_node  ->  . arithmetic_expression '*' arithmetic_leaf   (rule 78)
	arithmetic_node  ->  . arithmetic_expression '/' arithmetic_leaf   (rule 79)
	arithmetic_node  ->  . arithmetic_expression '^' arithmetic_leaf   (rule 80)
	arithmetic_leaf  ->  . '(' arithmetic_expression ')'   (rule 81)
	arithmetic_leaf  ->  . integer_value   (rule 82)
	arithmetic_leaf  ->  . real_value   (rule 83)
	arithmetic_leaf  ->  . absolute_path   (rule 84)
	absolute_path  ->  . '/'   (rule 85)
	absolute_path  ->  . '/' relative_path   (rule 86)
	absolute_path  ->  . absolute_path '/' relative_path   (rule 87)
	relative_path  ->  . path_segment   (rule 88)

	path_segment  ->  . V_ATTRIBUTE_IDENTIFIER V_LOCAL_TERM_CODE_REF   (rule 90)
	path_segment  ->  . V_ATTRIBUTE_IDENTIFIER   (rule 91)
	any_identifier  ->  . type_identifier   (rule 173)
	any_identifier  ->  . V_ATTRIBUTE_IDENTIFIER   (rule 174)
	type_identifier  ->  . '(' V_TYPE_IDENTIFIER ')'   (rule 175)
	type_identifier  ->  . '(' V_GENERIC_TYPE_IDENTIFIER ')'   (rule 176)
	type_identifier  ->  . V_TYPE_IDENTIFIER   (rule 177)
	type_identifier  ->  . V_GENERIC_TYPE_IDENTIFIER   (rule 178)
	integer_value  ->  . V_INTEGER   (rule 183)
	integer_value  ->  . '+' V_INTEGER   (rule 184)
	integer_value  ->  . '-' V_INTEGER   (rule 185)
	real_value  ->  . V_REAL   (rule 198)
	real_value  ->  . '+' V_REAL   (rule 199)
	real_value  ->  . '-' V_REAL   (rule 200)

	'('	shift, and go to state 1
	SYM_NOT	shift, and go to state 2
	'/'	shift, and go to state 3
	'-'	shift, and go to state 4
	'+'	shift, and go to state 5
	SYM_EXISTS	shift, and go to state 6
	SYM_FALSE	shift, and go to state 7
	SYM_TRUE	shift, and go to state 8
	V_ATTRIBUTE_IDENTIFIER	shift, and go to state 9
	V_GENERIC_TYPE_IDENTIFIER	shift, and go to state 10
	V_TYPE_IDENTIFIER	shift, and go to state 11
	V_REAL	shift, and go to state 12
	V_INTEGER	shift, and go to state 13

	$default	reduce using rule 49 (c_excludes)

	type_identifier	go to state 49
	absolute_path	go to state 17
	relative_path	go to state 18
	boolean_expression	go to state 19
	boolean_node	go to state 20
